commit e04db2f74238488bc7e384b07ecca2e71a328d48
Author: Aaron Fabbri <fabbri@cloudera.com>
Date:   Mon Dec 7 14:13:02 2015 -0800

    CPLAT-656 hadoop-aws shades old version of Joda-time, breaking S3A
    
    The cdh parent pom hard-codes an old version of joda-time, which was overriding
    the correct version required by the updated version of the aws-java-sdk-s3.
    
    Fix is to explicly specify the joda-time dependency with the version the current
    aws-java-sdk-s3 expects.
    
    This patch also fixes CDH-31245.

commit 5c3265cd09bb0cacc9e45ac431cdc0f17c4f24b4
Author: Aaron Fabbri <fabbri@cloudera.com>
Date:   Thu Jul 16 15:10:37 2015 -0700

    CDH-29426 CDH-29525 distcp to s3a fails due to integer overflow..
    
    Build fixes for newer AWS SDK.
    
    Fix classpath shading for joda-time.
    
    Excluding joda-time from the aws-java-sdk dependency breaks with newer versions
    of the aws sdk.
    
    In fact, the previous maven shading config was broken, because the shading
    relocation does nothing if that artifact is not a dependency.
    
    This commit adds the joda time classes to the uber/shaded jar, and adds
    depenency exclusions for the parent artifacts that depend on this one.

commit ef0e1ad4c687338b2a86b03882e1355dd7667f9d
Author: Mike Yoder <myoder@cloudera.com>
Date:   Tue Nov 3 14:35:25 2015 -0800

    CLOUDERA-BUILD. CDH-33705. HttpFS Keystore password exposed on cmd line
    
    The keystore password for httpfs was placed into $CATALINA_OPTS, which
    ultimately makes its way to the command line as Tomcat starts up. This
    changes things so that if CATALINA_BASE (the environment variable
    describing where Catalina config information is located) exists, and
    the catalina.properties file exists, then the appropriate config
    entries are written into the catalina.properties file. Information
    placed in that file goes into Tomcat just like the environment
    variable does.
    
    Change-Id: I7dfdc99fe6fbdbbec4ce04a6d46ad97d52eb6381
    (cherry picked from commit 77d25b45d3b6abea8fd0f7a9ba64bc32162c61f4)

commit 073fffec79bc0271bd1631057a585f9ef08fbd0a
Author: Gilad Wolff <gilad@cloudera.com>
Date:   Tue Jan 21 14:35:48 2014 -0800

    MR1: CLOUDERA-BUILD. Preliminary version of MAPREDUCE-5707. ApplicationClientProtocolPBClientImpl (and JobClient) does not allow to set rpcTimeout
    
    This commit adds the ability to enable rpc timeout for the job client.
    The approach taken was to add a new configuration parameter
    "mapreduce.jobclient.rpc.timeout". By default it is set to -1 (no
    timeout) to maintain backword compatibility. If set to some positive
    integer it will be used as the rpcTimeout in the underlying ipc Client.
    
    Testing done: New unit-tests. TestRpcTimeout hanged forever before
    this commit and now passes.
    (cherry-picked from commit 3167c63e253e502b16cfb27079d3bd825e96f4be)
    
    (cherry picked from commit 7901f25f833a93b17fb079e94f4f8ac57ee060d8)
